# Concern Plan: agent-runtime

**Tasks:** 1039
**Primary gate:** `roko parity gates lifecycle --strict`

## Execution Contract

- Use this file to batch related work, but update the checkbox in the source-specific plan file when implementation completes.
- Before coding, open every linked source-specific task because it contains the full source context and extracted details.
- Do not implement a cross-cutting concern in isolation without checking adjacent storage, auth, realtime, dashboard, and verification requirements.
- A task is done only when its source-specific acceptance criteria and this concern gate pass.

## Shared Checklist

- [ ] Runtime: wire into the production agent loop with lifecycle, cancellation, health, audit, provider/tool safety, and observable events.
